Data Preprocessing¶

In [3]:
def flatten_json(y):
    out = {}

    def flatten(x, name=''):
        if type(x) is dict:
            for a in x:
                flatten(x[a], name + a + '_')
        elif type(x) is list:
            i = 0
            for a in x:
                flatten(a, name + str(i) + '_')
                i += 1
        else:
            out[name[:-1]] = x

    flatten(y)
    return out
In [4]:
def getRow(x):
    if x is not np.nan:
        formatted = eval(x)
        return pd.json_normalize(flatten_json(formatted))
    return x

Dropping NaN¶

In [601]:
processed_lv_restaurant_df = lv_yelp_restaurant.copy(True)
processed_lv_restaurant_df = processed_lv_restaurant_df.dropna(subset=["hours"]).reset_index(drop=True)

Unnesting hours json in hours column¶

In [602]:
hours = processed_lv_restaurant_df["hours"].apply(getRow)
hours_df = hours[0]
for hour in hours[1:]:
    hours_df = pd.concat([hours_df, hour])
hours_df = hours_df.reset_index(drop=True)
In [603]:
processed_lv_restaurant_df = processed_lv_restaurant_df.join(hours_df)

date_lis = ['Monday', 'Tuesday', 'Wednesday',

    processed_lv_restaurant_df[date] = processed_lv_restaurant_df[date].str.split("-")
In [605]:
def get_restaurant_category(category):
    return processed_lv_restaurant_df[processed_lv_restaurant_df.categories.str.contains(category, regex=False)]
In [606]:
def convert_to_datetime(lis):
    if lis is not np.nan:
        return([datetime.strptime(lis[0], "%H:%M"), datetime.strptime(lis[1], "%H:%M")])
    return lis

# converting to datetime
for date in date_lis:
    processed_lv_restaurant_df[date] = processed_lv_restaurant_df[date].apply(convert_to_datetime)
In [607]:
def get_open_duration(time):
    # time is list type
    
    # returns a string in 24hr h:m:s format
    return str(time[1] - time[0])

def get_open_duration_second(time):
    return (time[1] - time[0]).seconds
In [608]:
def get_restaurant_price_range(attribute):
    if type(attribute) == str:
        attr_dict = eval(attribute)
        if "RestaurantsPriceRange2" not in attr_dict:
            return np.nan
        else:
            return int(attr_dict["RestaurantsPriceRange2"])

Cleaning empty space in categories¶

In [609]:
def strip_categories(text):
    return text.replace(" ", "")
processed_lv_restaurant_df.categories = processed_lv_restaurant_df.categories.apply(strip_categories)

In [641]:
def get_top_5_restaurant_per_category(category):
    # returns dict key: restaurant name value: yelp link
    top_5_restaurant = {}
    category_restaurant_df = get_restaurant_category(category)
    top_5 = category_restaurant_df.sort_values(by=["review_count", "stars"], ascending=False)[["name", "business_id"]].head()

    for i in range(len(top_5.name)):
        top_5_restaurant[top_5.name.iloc[i]] = f"https://www.yelp.com/biz/{top_5.business_id.iloc[i]}"
    return top_5_restaurant

Top Food Combination¶

In [425]:
def clean_categories(lis):
    return [x.strip() for x in lis]

def get_top_restaurant_per_category(category):
    category_restaurant_df = get_restaurant_category(category)
    return category_restaurant_df.sort_values(by=["review_count", "stars"], ascending=False)[:5]

categories_per_restaurant_record = list(processed_lv_restaurant_df.categories.str.split(",").apply(clean_categories))
result = apriori(categories_per_restaurant_record, min_support=0.0045, min_confidence=0.55, min_lift=3, min_length=3)
for item in result:

    # first index of the inner list
    # Contains base item and add item
    pair = item[0] 
    items = [x for x in pair]
    print("Rule: " + items[0] + " -> " + items[1])

    #second index of the inner list
    print("Support: " + str(item[1]))

    #third index of the list located at 0th
    #of the third index of the inner list

    print("Confidence: " + str(item[2][0][2]))
    print("Lift: " + str(item[2][0][3]))
    print("=====================================")

Common Food Combination for chosen Food Category¶

In [435]:
food_combination_category = {}
for food in top_10_food_category:
    
    category_df = get_top_restaurant_per_category(food)
    categories_list = list(x.categories.str.split(",").apply(clean_categories))
    rules = apriori(categories_list,  min_support=0.0045, min_confidence=0.55, min_lift=2,min_len=2)
    pattern_lis = []
    for item in rules:
        # first index of the inner list
        # Contains base item and add item
        pair = item[0] 
        items = [x for x in pair]
        pattern_lis.append(items[0] + " -> " + items[1])
    food_combination_category[food] = pattern_lis[:10]
    pattern_lis = []

def get_start_time(hours):
    return hours[0].hour
def get_end_time(hours):
    return hours[1].hour

Common Start time and End time for chosen food category¶

In [33]:
# key: category value: key:day value: time value count
starttime_category_dict = {}
endtime_category_dict = {}

for category in top_10_food_category:
    starttime_category_dict[category] = {}
    endtime_category_dict[category] = {}
    for day in day_lis:
        starttime_category_dict[category][day] = dict(get_restaurant_category(category)[day].dropna().apply(get_start_time).value_counts())
        endtime_category_dict[category][day] = dict(get_restaurant_category(category)[day].dropna().apply(get_end_time).value_counts())

sentiment_analyser = SentimentIntensityAnalyzer()
def vader_sentiment_analyzer_scores(sentence):
    score = sentiment_analyser.polarity_scores(sentence)
    return score

In [564]:
ml = MonkeyLearn('15853987b0638d766efa7ad144cc808e829abe27')
model_id = 'cl_pi3C7JiL'
def ml_sentiment_analyzer_scores(ml, model_id, text):
    data = [text]
    result = ml.classifiers.classify(model_id, data)
    return f"[{result.body[0]['classifications'][0]['tag_name']}: {result.body[0]['classifications'][0]['confidence']}]"

Key Word Extractor¶

In [205]:
def ml_keyword_extractor(ml, data):
    # return dict with key: keyword value: relevance to text
    parsed_keyword = ml.extractors.extract('ex_YCya9nrn', [data]).body[0]["extractions"]
    key_word = {}
    for extracted in parsed_keyword:
        key_word[extracted["parsed_value"]] = float(extracted["relevance"])
    return parsed_keyword

Common Phrases¶

In [514]:
quality_reviews = lv_yelp_restaurant_review[((lv_yelp_restaurant_review.useful>0) | (lv_yelp_restaurant_review.funny > 0) | (lv_yelp_restaurant_review.cool> 0))]
quality_reviews =quality_reviews.set_index("business_id").join(processed_lv_restaurant_df.set_index("business_id")[["categories"]], how="inner")
quality_reviews["review_quality"] = quality_reviews.useful+quality_reviews.funny+quality_reviews.cool

quality_tips =lv_yelp_restaurant_tip[lv_yelp_restaurant_tip.compliment_count > 0]
quality_tips = quality_tips.set_index("business_id").join(processed_lv_restaurant_df.set_index("business_id")[["categories"]], how="inner")

processed_quality_tips = quality_tips[["text"]]
processed_quality_review_df = pd.concat([quality_reviews[["text"]], processed_quality_tips])
In [505]:
def get_category(df, category):
    if category is not None:
        t = df.reset_index()
        return t[t.categories.str.contains(category, regex=False)]
    return df
In [383]:
def is_english_text(review):
    if TextBlob(review).detect_language() == 'en':
        return True
    else:
        return False
def clean_review(review):
    text = review.lower()
    return re.sub(r"(food)|(restaurant)|(vegas)|(place)|(order)", "", text)
def get_sample_review(df, number):
    return df.sample(number)["text"].apply(clean_review)
In [385]:
def get_keyword(ml, data):
    # return dict with key: keyword value: relevance to text
    parsed_keyword = ml.extractors.extract('ex_YCya9nrn', [data]).body[0]["extractions"]
    key_word = {}
    for extracted in parsed_keyword:
        key_word[extracted["parsed_value"]] = float(extracted["relevance"])
    return key_word

Get Context of Phrase¶

In [580]:
def get_context(phrase, category=None):
    # returns a dict with the context from review and tip
    
    context_dict = {"review":{}, "tip": {}}
    filtered_reviews = get_category(quality_reviews, category)
    filtered_tips = get_category(quality_tips, category)
    
    top_review = filtered_reviews[filtered_reviews.text.str.lower().str.contains(phrase)].sort_values(["review_quality"], ascending=False)
    top_tip = filtered_tips[filtered_tips.text.str.lower().str.contains(phrase)]
    
    # if there is no tip
    if len(top_tip) != 0:
        print("inside")
        top_tip = top_tip.sort_values(["compliment_count"], ascending=False).iloc[0, :]
    
    review_col = ["stars", "useful", "funny", "cool", "text"]
    tip_col = ["text"]
    
    for review_attr in review_col:
        context_dict["review"][review_attr] = top_review.iloc[0, :][review_attr]
    context_dict["review"]["sentiment_analysis"] = ml_sentiment_analyzer_scores(ml, model_id, top_review.iloc[0,:]["text"])
    
    if len(top_tip) == 0:
        # the tip becomes another review
        for review_attr in review_col:
            context_dict["tip"][review_attr] = top_review.iloc[1, :][review_attr]
        context_dict["tip"]["sentiment_analysis"] = ml_sentiment_analyzer_scores(ml, model_id, top_review.iloc[1,:]["text"])
    else:
        for tip_attr in tip_col:
            context_dict["tip"][tip_attr] = top_tip[tip_attr]
        context_dict["tip"]["sentiment_analysis"] = ml_sentiment_analyzer_scores(ml, model_id, top_tip["text"])
    return context_dict

Phrase Context¶

In [ ]:
context_phrase = {"General": {}, "Category":{}}
for phrase in common_phrase:
    context_phrase["General"][phrase] = get_context(phrase)
In [565]:
for category in common_phrase_category:
    context_phrase["Category"][category] = {}
    for phrase in common_phrase_category[category]:
        context_phrase["Category"][category][phrase] = get_context(phrase, category)
